I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the ground truth:

**GT: c0*P*sin(c1*t) + c2*P*exp(-c3*t)**

where c0Ōēł0.257, c1Ōēł0.722, c2Ōēł0.115, c3Ōēł0.030.

The GT has two terms, both proportional to P:
1. P*sin(c1*t) ŌĆö oscillatory term
2. P*exp(-c3*t) ŌĆö exponential decay term

Let me analyze each candidate:

### Candidate 1: P*c0*cos(c1*t + c2) + P*c3 + P*c4 + P**c5*c6
- P*cos(c1*t+c2) can represent P*sin(c1*t) via phase shift (c2 = ŽĆ/2)
- P*(c3+c4) gives a constant├ŚP term
- P**c5*c6: if c5=1, this adds another constant├ŚP; total is P*cos(c1*t+c2) + P*const
- But GT has P*exp(-c3*t), not a constant P term. A constant cannot match exp(-c3*t) for all t.
- **Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 2: P┬▓*c0 + P┬▓*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3*log(c4/(P+c5)+1) + P*c6*cos(c7*t+c8)
- Has P┬▓ terms (set c0=c1=0), P*c2 constant, P*log(...) depends on P not t, P*cos(c7*t+c8) oscillatory
- Missing exp(-c3*t) dependence on t. The log term depends on P, not t.
